22/09/23, 5:40â€¯pm - +91 81010 61561: The term "Father of Democracy" is often attributed to Cleisthenes, an ancient Athenian statesman, for his significant reforms that laid the foundation for Athenian democracy around 507-508 BCE. As for the "Mother of Democracy," this is a less common title, but sometimes it's used metaphorically to refer to Athena, the Greek goddess of wisdom and warfare, as Athens, the birthplace of democracy, was named after her. These titles are symbolic and not meant to be taken literally.

13/04/24, 3:04â€¯pm - Purnendu Kumar Misra: @916297127251 and many were asking for how to access the server form personal laptop. Here is the solution-

(I am assuming you are on windows)
1. Open command prompt
2. Type ssh username@172.16.4.112
3. Press enter
4. If you are doing it for the 1st time, it will ask for yes/no/fingerprint -> just type yes and press enter
5. Then enter the password and press enter.
6. You will be in server and then the next commands will be same as you do in labs like vi, cd...

29/08/24, 11:28â€¯am - Aditya: Exercise 1Â -Â Introduction to OpenstackRead the Wikipedia entry for Openstack. Specifically, make sure that you understand
a) What is Openstack (Introduction).
OpenStack is a free and open-source software platform for cloud computing, mostly deployed as IaaS, whereby virtual servers and other resources are made available to customers. The software platform consists of interrelated components that control diverse, multi-vendor hardware pools of processing, storage, and networking resources throughout a data center.
b) Identify which level of virtualization it provides (SaaS, PaaS, IaaS, any other XaaS?)
As we said before, it provides IaaS (infrastructure-as-a-service).
c) The role of each one of the components.

â€¢ - Â Compute (Nova): is a cloud computing fabric controller. It is designed to manage and automate pools of computer resources and can work with a widely available virtualization technologies. Scaling has become an increasingly important issue.
â€¢ - Â Networking (Neutron): is a system for managing networks and IP addresses.
â€¢ - Â Block Storage (Cinder): provides persistent block-level storage devices for use with OpenStack compute instances. This system manages the creation, attaching and detaching of the block devices to servers.
â€¢ - Â Identity (Keystone): provides a central directory of users mapped to the OpenStack services they can access. It acts as a common authentication system across the cloud operating system.
â€¢ - Â Image (Glance): provides discovery, registration and delivery services for disk and server images.
â€¢ - Â Object Storage (Swift): is a scalable redundant storage system.
â€¢ - Â Dashboard (Horizon): provides administrators and users with a graphical interface to access, provision, and automate deployment of cloud-based resources.
â€¢ - Â Orchestration (Heat): is a service to orchestrate multiple composite cloud applications using templates, through both an OpenStack-native REST API and a CloudFormation-compatible Query API.
â€¢ - Â Workflow (Mistral): is a service that manage workflows.
â€¢ - Â Telemetry (Ceilometer):Â â€‹provides a Single Point Of Contact for billing systems, providing all the counters they need to establish customer billing, across all current and future OpenStack components.
â€¢ - Â Database (Trove): iâ€‹s a database-as-a-service provisioningÂ â€‹relational and a non-relational dâ€‹Â atabaseâ€‹Â engine.
â€¢ - Â Elastic map reduce (Sahara) : is a component to easily and rapidly provisionÂ â€‹Hadoop clusters.
â€¢ - Â Bare metal (Ironic):Â is an OpenStack project that provisions bare metal machines instead of virtual machines.
â€¢ - Â Messaging (Zaqar):Â iâ€‹Â s a multi-tenant cloud messaging service for Web developers.
â€¢ - Â Shared file system (Manila):Â â€‹provides an open API to manage shares in a vendorÂ agnostic framework.
â€¢ - Â DNS(Designate):iâ€‹samulti-tenantRESTAPIformanagingDNS.
â€¢ - Â Search (Searchlight):Â pâ€‹Â rovides advanced and consistent search capabilities across various OpenStack cloud services.
â€¢ - Â Key Manager (Barbican):Â iâ€‹s a REST API designed for the secure storage, provisioning and management of secrets.
â€¢ - Â Container orchestration (Magnum):Â â€‹is an OpenStack API service developed by the OpenStack Containers Team making container orchestration engines such as Docker Swarm, Kubernetes, and Apache Mesos available as first class resources in OpenStack.
â€¢ - Â Root Cause Analysis (Vitrage):Â iâ€‹Â s the OpenStack RCA (Root Cause Analysis) service for organizing, analyzing and expanding OpenStack alarms & events, yielding insights regarding the root cause of problems and deducing their existence before they are directly detected.
â€¢ - Â Rule-based alarm actions (Aodh):Â Tâ€‹Â his alarming service enables the ability to trigger actions based on defined rules against metric or event data collected by Ceilometer or Gnocchi.

d) What are the mandatory components for the simplest deployment?
The mandatory components are dashboard, compute, networking, identity, Image Service, Object Storage, block Storage and Telemetry.
